CC   -!- FUNCTION: Glucanases play a role in cell expansion during growth,
CC       in cell-cell fusion during mating, and in spore release during
CC       sporulation. This enzyme may be involved in beta-glucan
CC       degradation and also function biosynthetically as a
CC       transglycosylase (By similarity). {ECO:0000250}.
CC   -!- CATALYTIC ACTIVITY: Hydrolysis of (1->3)-beta-D-glucosidic
CC       linkages in (1->3)-beta-D-glucans.
CC   -!- SUBCELLULAR LOCATION: Cell membrane {ECO:0000250}; Lipid-anchor,
CC       GPI-anchor {ECO:0000250}. Secreted, cell wall {ECO:0000250}.
CC       Note=Covalently-linked GPI-modified cell wall protein.
CC       {ECO:0000250}.
CC   -!- PTM: The GPI-anchor is attached to the protein in the endoplasmic
CC       reticulum and serves to target the protein to the cell surface.
CC       There, the glucosamine-inositol phospholipid moiety is cleaved off
CC       and the GPI-modified mannoprotein is covalently attached via its
CC       lipidless GPI glycan remnant to the 1,6-beta-glucan of the outer
CC       cell wall layer (By similarity). {ECO:0000250}.
CC   -!- SIMILARITY: Belongs to the glycosyl hydrolase 17 family.
CC       {ECO:0000305}.

CC       transglycosylase. {ECO:0000269|PubMed:15950156}.

CC       cell wall {ECO:0000269|PubMed:19585695}. Note=Covalently-linked
CC       GPI-modified cell wall protein.
CC   -!- INDUCTION: Expression is under the control of the nsdD
CC       transcription factor required for sexual development. Transcript
CC       level is the highest at the beginning of asexual development and
CC       decreases thereafter to increase again at the late stage.
CC       {ECO:0000269|PubMed:15950156}.
CC   -!- PTM: The GPI-anchor is attached to the protein in the endoplasmic
CC       reticulum and serves to target the protein to the cell surface.
CC       There, the glucosamine-inositol phospholipid moiety is cleaved off
CC       and the GPI-modified mannoprotein is covalently attached via its
CC       lipidless GPI glycan remnant to the 1,6-beta-glucan of the outer
CC       cell wall layer (By similarity). {ECO:0000250}.

CC       {ECO:0000250}.
CC   -!- PTM: The GPI-anchor is attached to the protein in the endoplasmic

CC       and the GPI-modified mannoprotein is covalently attached via its
CC       lipidless GPI glycan remnant to the 1,6-beta-glucan of the outer

CC   -!- FUNCTION: Transcriptional activator of the xylanolytic system.
CC       Involved in the regulation of extracellular cellulolytic and
CC       xylanolytic genes and in the regulation of the intracellular
CC       activities of D-xylose catabolic genes in the pentose catabolic
CC       pathway (PCP) in response to the presence of D-xylose. Binds to
CC       the DNA sequence 5'-GGNTAAA-3'. {ECO:0000269|PubMed:10508057,
CC       ECO:0000269|PubMed:10760176, ECO:0000269|PubMed:11916668,
CC       ECO:0000269|PubMed:12242504, ECO:0000269|PubMed:17951513,
CC       ECO:0000269|PubMed:18332432, ECO:0000269|PubMed:21484208,
CC       ECO:0000269|PubMed:21892241, ECO:0000269|PubMed:9758775,
CC       ECO:0000269|Ref.8}.
CC   -!- SUBCELLULAR LOCATION: Nucleus.
CC   -!- INDUCTION: Expressed in presence of xylose.
CC       {ECO:0000269|PubMed:18332432}.
CC   -!- DISRUPTION PHENOTYPE: Reduces growth on birchwod xylan, while
CC       growth is unaffected on D-xylose, xylitol and other carbon sources
CC       like D-glucose, L-arabinose or L-arabitol.
CC       {ECO:0000269|PubMed:21892241, ECO:0000269|Ref.8}.
